                             ===Evaluation Report===                                                                                                                                                             
                             # Evaluation Report                                                                                                                                                                 
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             ## Summary                                                                                                                                                                          
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             A stack-based buffer overflow was detected in the function `mg_json_get` (in `src/mongoose/src/json.c`). When invoked via the fuzzing harness, AddressSanitizer                     
                             reports a one-byte write beyond the bounds of a fixed-size local array named `nesting`. The overflow is triggered by the fuzz test entry point in                                   
                             `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` within `src/mongoose/test/fuzz.c`.                                                                                                                         
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             ## Description                                                                                                                                                                      
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             - Issue overview                                                                                                                                                                    
                               AddressSanitizer flagged a stack-buffer-overflow in `mg_json_get` at line 186 of `json.c`. The vulnerable frame contains a local array `nesting` with a                           
                             compile-time size of 32 bytes, but the code writes to index 62, overrunning the buffer.                                                                                             
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             - Vulnerability type                                                                                                                                                                
                               This is a classic stack-based buffer overflow, classified by AddressSanitizer as 1-byte-write-stack-buffer-overflow.                                                            
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             - Key observations                                                                                                                                                                  
                                The overflow occurs in the JSON lookup routine `mg_json_get`.                                                                                                                   
                                The stack frame shows `nesting` declared at lines 127131 in `json.c`.                                                                                                          
                                The corrupted write happens at line 186, indicating insufficient bounds checking on the nesting depth or index.                                                                 
                                The bug was discovered by running the libFuzzer harness (`LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` at `fuzz.c:81`) with one test input invoked 100 times.                                        
                                The sanitizer output includes the relevant call stack from the fuzzer driver through `Fuzzer::ExecuteCallback`.                                                                 
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             - Code areas to investigate                                                                                                                                                         
                               1. `src/mongoose/src/json.c`                                                                                                                                                      
                                   Definition and size of the `nesting` array (around line 127).                                                                                                                
                                   Code paths in `mg_json_get` that index into `nesting` (around line 186).                                                                                                     
                               2. The fuzzing harness in `src/mongoose/test/fuzz.c` (around line 81) to understand how inputs flow into `mg_json_get`.                                                           
                               3. Any JSON parsing or lookup utility functions called by `mg_json_get` that manipulate the `nesting` buffer.                                                                     
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             Investigating these locations will provide a holistic view of how inputs lead to the overflow and what checks (if any) are missing around the nesting buffer.

                             ===Evaluation Report===                                                                                                                                                             
                             # Evaluation Report                                                                                                                                                                 
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             ## Summary                                                                                                                                                                          
                             The initial issue is an AddressSanitizer stack-buffer-overflow in the function `mg_json_get` (src/mongoose/src/json.c:186), triggered by the fuzzer harness in                      
                             `test/fuzz.c`. The overflow writes one byte past the end of the local array `nesting` (declared around line 131).                                                                   
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             A patch attempt changed two checks from `if (depth > MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING)` to `if (depth >= MG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH)` in the object (`{`) and array (`[`) handling                        
                             branches of `mg_json_get`. After applying this patch, the same stack-buffer-overflow persists at the same code location, as confirmed by the repeated ASan report.                  
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             ## Description                                                                                                                                                                      
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             Initial issue                                                                                                                                                                       
                             - While running the libFuzzer-based test harness (`LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` in test/fuzz.c) against `mg_json_get`, AddressSanitizer reports a 1-byte write past the                  
                             end of the stack-allocated array `nesting`.                                                                                                                                         
                             - The overflow is detected at `json.c:186:28` inside `mg_json_get`. The shadow-byte dump shows the write touches the redzone immediately following the `nesting`                    
                             array (offset 62 into a buffer sized 30 bytes, indicating a boundary violation).                                                                                                    
                             - Stack frame information points to a single local object:                                                                                                                          
                                  `nesting`, declared on line 131 of `src/json.c`, spans bytes [32, 62) in the frame, but code writes at offset 62.                                                             
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             Patch attempt                                                                                                                                                                       
                             - In `src/json.c`, two adjacent code blocks handling JSON object `{` and array `[` tokens were altered:                                                                             
                                  Original checks:                                                                                                                                                              
                                     if (depth > MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING) return MG_JSON_TOO_DEEP;                                                                                                                   
                                  Patched checks:                                                                                                                                                               
                                     if (depth >= MG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH) return MG_JSON_TOO_DEEP;                                                                                                                    
                             - No other changes were made to the logic that increments or indexes into `nesting`.                                                                                                
                             - After rebuilding and re-running the fuzzer for 100 iterations, the same AddressSanitizer stack-buffer-overflow occurs at the identical code location in                           
                             `mg_json_get`.                                                                                                                                                                      
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             Log after patch                                                                                                                                                                     
                             - ASan emits the same WRITE of size 1 at  stack-buffer-overflow message.                                                                                                         
                             - The stack and shadow-byte diagnostics are unchanged, confirming the overflow remains unaddressed.                                                                                 
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             Areas requiring further inspection                                                                                                                                                  
                             - The definition and sizing of the local array `nesting` in `mg_json_get` (around line 131). Verify its capacity versus the maximum possible `depth` values.                        
                             - The macros `MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING` and `MG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH` and how they relate to the declared length of `nesting`.                                                                 
                             - The loops and index manipulations in `mg_json_get` that advance the `depth` counter and write into `nesting`.                                                                     
                             - The code path in `test/fuzz.c` (the fuzzer entry point) to understand input patterns that trigger deep nesting or unexpected index values.                                        
                             - Surrounding JSON parsing logic in `json.c` for consistency between bound checks and actual buffer sizes.                                                                          
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             No speculation on root causes or fixes is provided. The report focuses on observed behavior before and after the patch and identifies code regions for deeper                       
                             review.

                             ## Fix Strategy                                                                                                                                                                     
                             <fix_strategy>                                                                                                                                                                      
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             1. Understand the root cause:                                                                                                                                                       
                                - The local array `nesting` in mg_json_get is sized by `MG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH` (30), yet the code was guarding against `MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING` (60). This allowed                      
                             `depth` to grow up to 59 before the check, causing writes at `nesting[30]nesting[59]` and overflowing.                                                                             
                                - The last patch changed the wrong macro references in two branches, but it did **not** mirror the proven guard used in patched test code (`if (depth >=                         
                             sizeof(nesting))`) and may not have applied the change at every write site.                                                                                                         
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             2. Locate **all** write sites into `nesting[]`:                                                                                                                                     
                                - Within the `S_VALUE` state: when encountering `{`, after the guard, the code does `nesting[depth++] = c;`.                                                                     
                                - Similarly, for `[`, it does `nesting[depth++] = c;`.                                                                                                                           
                                - Outside of those branches, there is Symmetry on the `}` and `]` sides: they decrement `depth` and write into `nesting` via other logic (e.g., when closing an                  
                             object or array, the code advances positions in `path`).                                                                                                                            
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             3. Amend the guards comprehensively:                                                                                                                                                
                                - Replace **both** occurrences of                                                                                                                                                
                                    `if (depth > MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING) return MG_JSON_TOO_DEEP;`                                                                                                                  
                                  with                                                                                                                                                                           
                                    `if (depth >= MG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH) return MG_JSON_TOO_DEEP;`                                                                                                                   
                                  **and** ensure these guards occur **immediately before** each `nesting[depth++] = ` write. This ensures that the maximum valid `depth` is `MG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH                  
                             - 1`.                                                                                                                                                                               
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             4. Use the proven pattern from patched test code:                                                                                                                                   
                                - Instead of relying on the macros (which can drift), directly guard against the actual array size:                                                                              
                                    `if (depth >= (int) (sizeof(nesting) / sizeof(nesting[0])))`                                                                                                                 
                                  This ties the bound check to the actual buffer size, preventing future mismatches if macros change.                                                                            
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             5. Implementation steps in `src/json.c`:                                                                                                                                            
                                a. At the `{` branch:                                                                                                                                                            
                                   - Before `nesting[depth++] = c;`, insert or replace the guard with:                                                                                                           
                                       `if (depth >= (int) (sizeof(nesting) / sizeof(nesting[0])))`                                                                                                              
                                           `return MG_JSON_TOO_DEEP;`                                                                                                                                            
                                b. At the `[` branch:                                                                                                                                                            
                                   - Analogous change before `nesting[depth++] = c;`.                                                                                                                            
                                c. Confirm no other writes into `nesting` elsewhere without similar guards.                                                                                                      
                                d. Remove references to `MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING` entirely in this function (or deprecate it), using only the `sizeof(nesting)` check to avoid redundancy.                           
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             6. Preserve existing functionality:                                                                                                                                                 
                                - All other parsing logic remains intact (updates to `ed`, `pos`, `ci`, `ei`, and state transitions).                                                                            
                                - The fuzzer harness and tests unmodified; the guard change is local to `json.c`.                                                                                                
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             7. Validate:                                                                                                                                                                        
                                - Rebuild and run the fuzzer 100+ iterations to confirm the stack-buffer-overflow is gone.                                                                                       
                                - Run the full test suite to ensure no regressions.                                                                                                                              
                                - Optionally, add a unit test that constructs a JSON string with exactly 30 levels of nested objects/arrays and verifies `mg_json_get` returns                                   
                             `MG_JSON_TOO_DEEP` at the 31st level.                                                                                                                                               
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             Justification:                                                                                                                                                                      
                             - Tying the depth guard directly to `sizeof(nesting)` ensures consistency between the buffer size and the permitted index range, eliminating the previous macro                     
                             mismatch.                                                                                                                                                                           
                             - This localized change does not affect any external APIs, harness, or tests.                                                                                                       
                             - The approach mirrors the working patch in the test scaffold and prevents any future off-by-one or macro-drift errors.                                                             
                             - Potential side effect: if someone changes `MG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH`, the guard auto-adjusts; no additional macro edits are needed.                                                      
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             </fix_strategy>                                                                                                                                                                     
                             ===Evaluation End===

                             ===Evaluation Report===                                                                                                                                                             
                             # Evaluation Report                                                                                                                                                                 
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             ## Summary                                                                                                                                                                          
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             The codebases JSON helper function `mg_json_get` exhibits a one-byte stack-buffer overflow when exercised by the libFuzzer harness. The overflow occurs in the                     
                             local array `nesting[]` when its index `depth` exceeds the arrays bounds.                                                                                                          
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             An attempted patch replaced checks against `MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING` with comparisons to the actual `sizeof(nesting) / sizeof(nesting[0])`. After applying this change,                 
                             repeated fuzzing still triggers the same AddressSanitizer stack-buffer-overflow at the same location in `mg_json_get`.                                                              
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             ## Description                                                                                                                                                                      
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             1. Initial Issue                                                                                                                                                                    
                                - During a libFuzzer run, AddressSanitizer reports a stack-buffer-overflow inside `mg_json_get` (in `src/json.c`, around line 186).                                              
                                - The overflow writes one byte just past the end of the local `nesting` array.                                                                                                   
                                - The crash log pinpoints the overflow as a write to offset 62 of a buffer that spans only indices [0,31] (32 bytes).                                                            
                                - The fuzzer entry point is `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` in `test/fuzz.c`, which invokes `mg_json_get` on arbitrary input paths.                                                     
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             2. Patch Attempt                                                                                                                                                                    
                                - In `src/json.c`, two conditionals guarding entry into `{` and `[` contexts were changed:                                                                                       
                                  * Old: `if (depth > MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING) return MG_JSON_TOO_DEEP;`                                                                                                             
                                  * New: `if (depth >= (int)(sizeof(nesting) / sizeof(nesting[0]))) return MG_JSON_TOO_DEEP;`                                                                                    
                                - This aligns the guard with the actual size of `nesting`, instead of an independent constant `MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING`.                                                             
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             3. Patch Result                                                                                                                                                                     
                                - After rebuilding and rerunning the same fuzz harness, AddressSanitizer reports the identical buffer overflow at the same instruction (`json.c:186`).                           
                                - The shadow-byte diagnostics are unchanged, confirming the out-of-bounds write still occurs at stack offset 62.                                                                 
                                - The fuzzer log (new seed) still reports the crash under the same call stack, with `mg_json_get` as the faulty frame.                                                           
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             4. Areas for Further Investigation                                                                                                                                                  
                                - The logic in `mg_json_get` that increments or uses the `depth` variable and assigns into `nesting[depth]`.                                                                     
                                - The relationship between `MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING` and the actual size of the `nesting` array.                                                                                     
                                - All code paths in `mg_json_get` that manipulate `depth` and index into `nesting`, especially around object (`{`) and array (`[`) handling and path parsing.                    
                                - Any other uses of fixed-size local arrays driven by parsed input, to check for similar or related bounds-checking gaps.

                             ## Fix Strategy                                                                                                                                                                     
                             <fix_strategy>                                                                                                                                                                      
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             1. Root Cause Analysis                                                                                                                                                              
                                - The stack-buffer-overflow in `mg_json_get` stems from a mismatch between the compile-time size of the local array `nesting[]` and the run-time limit used to                   
                             guard its writes.                                                                                                                                                                   
                                - The array is declared as `unsigned char nesting[MG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH]` (default 30), while the code permits up to `MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING` levels (default 60)                       
                             before bailing out. Thus, when `depth` climbs into [30..59], the code happily writes past the end of `nesting`, corrupting the stack.                                               
                                - Previous patch attempts tweaked the guard to compare against `sizeof(nesting)`, but because `nesting` was still size 30, deeper inputs (depth  30) still                      
                             caused out-of-bounds writes at the same instruction.                                                                                                                                
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             2. Strategy Overview                                                                                                                                                                
                                To eliminate the overflow without altering the fuzz harness or external tests, we must ensure that the in-scope buffer is at least as large as the deepest                       
                             nesting the code intends to support. We choose to make `nesting[]` use `MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING` so that its capacity and its guards align perfectly.                                   
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             3. Detailed Steps                                                                                                                                                                   
                                A. In `src/json.c`, locate the declaration of `nesting`:                                                                                                                         
                                   ```c                                                                                                                                                                          
                                   unsigned char nesting[MG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH];                                                                                                                                     
                                   ```                                                                                                                                                                           
                                   Change it to:                                                                                                                                                                 
                                   ```c                                                                                                                                                                          
                                   unsigned char nesting[MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING];                                                                                                                                   
                                   ```                                                                                                                                                                           
                                   This expands the buffer to the full depth the runtime checks already allow (default 60).                                                                                      
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                                B. In the same function, unify the depth-check guards to use the arrays actual size. Replace both occurrences of:                                                               
                                   ```c                                                                                                                                                                          
                                   if (depth > MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING) return MG_JSON_TOO_DEEP;                                                                                                                     
                                   ```                                                                                                                                                                           
                                   with:                                                                                                                                                                         
                                   ```c                                                                                                                                                                          
                                   if (depth >= (int)(sizeof(nesting) / sizeof(nesting[0]))) return MG_JSON_TOO_DEEP;                                                                                            
                                   ```                                                                                                                                                                           
                                   This ensures the code never writes beyond the end of `nesting[]`, regardless of how the macros evolve in the future.                                                          
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                                C. (Optional but recommended) Add a `static_assert` in `json.h` or at the top of `json.c` to guarantee that `MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING` remains a reasonable                           
                             compile-time constant (e.g., not negative or zero):                                                                                                                                 
                                   ```c                                                                                                                                                                          
                                   _Static_assert(MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING > 0, "MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING must be positive");                                                                                              
                                   ```                                                                                                                                                                           
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             4. Preservation of Existing Logic                                                                                                                                                   
                                - We do not change any semantics of nesting or path parsing: the code still allows the same maximum nesting (`MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING`) before returning                             
                             `MG_JSON_TOO_DEEP`.                                                                                                                                                                 
                                - No harness or fuzzing logic is touched, so all existing tests and fuzz targets continue to operate unchanged.                                                                  
                                - We avoid broadening or narrowing error conditions: only buffer capacity is adjusted to match the intended guard.                                                               
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             5. Why This Is Optimal                                                                                                                                                              
                                - Directly aligns buffer capacity with the existing guard, eliminating the root cause of overflow.                                                                               
                                - Minimal impact: only a single line change to the declaration plus two guard updates in one function.                                                                           
                                - Future-proof: by using `sizeof(nesting)` in checks, we auto-adapt if someone later tweaks the macros.                                                                          
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             6. Potential Side Effects & Mitigations                                                                                                                                             
                                - The stack frame size for `mg_json_get` will grow by `(MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING - MG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH)` bytes (default +30 bytes). This is negligible in this context.                 
                                - If downstream code expected to cap at 30 levels, they will now allow 60. However, since the original guard already allowed 60, this is merely restoring                        
                             intended behavior.                                                                                                                                                                  
                                - Should any caller rely on `MG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH` being the true maximum, they will need to switch to `MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING` for clarity; consider cleaning up                      
                             deprecated macros later.                                                                                                                                                            
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             </fix_strategy>

                             ===Evaluation Report===                                                                                                                                                             
                             # Evaluation Report                                                                                                                                                                 
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             ## Summary                                                                                                                                                                          
                             The initial issue arises when the fuzzing harness invokes the function `mg_json_get` in mongooses JSON parser, triggering an AddressSanitizer                                      
                             stack-buffer-overflow. The overflow occurs because a local array `nesting` is written one byte past its allocated size.                                                             
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             A patch attempt was made in `src/json.c` to (1) change the declaration of `nesting` from `unsigned char nesting[MG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH]` to `unsigned char                               
                             nesting[MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING]`, and (2) tighten boundary checks on entering `{` or `[` by comparing `depth` against the actual size of `nesting` via                                 
                             `sizeof(nesting)`.                                                                                                                                                                  
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             When the patched code was re-fuzzed, the same sanitizer error recurred at the same stack location, indicating that the overflow has not been eliminated by the                      
                             changes.                                                                                                                                                                            
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             ## Description                                                                                                                                                                      
                             1. Initial Issue                                                                                                                                                                    
                                - The fuzzer input triggers a one-byte write beyond the `nesting` array in `mg_json_get`.                                                                                        
                                - AddressSanitizer reports the overflow at offset 62 in the stack frame, corresponding to the `nesting` buffer (which spans bytes [32,62)).                                      
                                - The crash stack trace points to line 186 in `json.c` (inside `mg_json_get`) where a write addresses `nesting[depth]` without adequate bounds checking.                         
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             2. Key Observations in the Initial Log                                                                                                                                              
                                - The local array `nesting` is sized according to `MG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH`.                                                                                                           
                                - A code path increments `depth` when seeing `{` or `[`, but does not prevent `depth` from reaching the arrays length before writing.                                           
                                - The error is reproducible under libFuzzer with a simple invocation (`/out/fuzz  /testcase`).                                                                                  
                                - The sanitizer report shows 1-byte-write-stack-buffer-overflow in `mg_json_get:186:28`, and labels the affected area as the `nesting` variable.                               
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             3. Patch Attempt Details                                                                                                                                                            
                                - File modified: `src/json.c`.                                                                                                                                                   
                                - Change 1 (line 127):                                                                                                                                                           
                                  ```diff                                                                                                                                                                        
                                  - unsigned char nesting[MG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH];                                                                                                                                    
                                  + unsigned char nesting[MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING];                                                                                                                                  
                                  ```                                                                                                                                                                            
                                - Change 2 (around line 164):                                                                                                                                                    
                                  ```diff                                                                                                                                                                        
                                  - if (depth > MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING) return MG_JSON_TOO_DEEP;                                                                                                                    
                                  + if (depth >= (int)(sizeof(nesting)/sizeof(nesting[0]))) return MG_JSON_TOO_DEEP;                                                                                             
                                  ```                                                                                                                                                                            
                                - Change 3 (around line 173): same as Change 2 but for `[` handling.                                                                                                             
                                - Rationale: replace the original constant with a new one and use the actual array size for bounds checking.                                                                     
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             4. Post-Patch Log and Findings                                                                                                                                                      
                                - The fuzzer run under the same conditions still reports a stack-buffer-overflow at the same address and stack frame.                                                            
                                - The sanitizer notes writing at offset 62 in `nesting` (bytes [32,62)) remains out of bounds.                                                                                   
                                - No change in crash location or error message indicates that the new checks and array size did not prevent the overflow.                                                        
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             5. Areas for Further Investigation                                                                                                                                                  
                                - Verify the values and relationship of `MG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH` vs. `MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING` constants to ensure the array is actually enlarged.                                        
                                - Audit all increments and writes to `nesting[depth]` in `mg_json_get` to confirm that `depth` can never equal the array length before a write.                                  
                                - Examine any loops or recursive calls in `mg_json_get` that modify `depth` or use `nesting` for additional overflow opportunities.                                              
                                - Review surrounding code that computes or modifies `depth` and `ed` (expected depth) to understand legitimate maximum values in pathological inputs.                            
                                - Consider other local buffers or variables in the same function that might contribute to indexing errors under fuzzed inputs.

                             ===Evaluation Report===                                                                                                                                                             
                             # Evaluation Report                                                                                                                                                                 
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             ## Summary                                                                                                                                                                          
                             - Initial issue: When running the fuzzer against the `mg_json_get` function in `src/mongoose/src/json.c`, AddressSanitizer reports a one-byte                                       
                             stack-buffer-overflow. The local array `nesting[]` is allocated for a limited number of nesting levels but is written past its end (offset 62), causing the crash.                  
                             - Patch attempt:                                                                                                                                                                    
                                In `src/json.h`, the defaults for `MG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH` and `MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING` were reordered and `MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING` was increased from 30 to 60.                           
                                In `src/json.c`, the checks before entering a new object (`{`) or array (`[`) were changed to compare `depth+1` against the actual size of the `nesting` array                  
                             (`sizeof(nesting)/sizeof(nesting[0])`) instead of the macro `MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING`.                                                                                                  
                             - Patch result: Fuzzing after the patch still triggers the same AddressSanitizer error in `mg_json_get` at line 186, indicating that the write beyond the `nesting`                 
                             array remains unmitigated.                                                                                                                                                          
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             ## Description                                                                                                                                                                      
                             1. Initial issue details                                                                                                                                                            
                                - Fuzzer invocation: libFuzzer runs `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput`, which calls `mg_json_get` via a test harness in `test/fuzz.c`.                                                     
                                - Crash signature:                                                                                                                                                               
                                   Error: `AddressSanitizer: stack-buffer-overflow`                                                                                                                             
                                   Faulting write: 1-byte write at address corresponding to `nesting[depth]`, where `depth` reached 62.                                                                         
                                   Vulnerable frame:                                                                                                                                                            
                                     Function: `mg_json_get` in `json.c`                                                                                                                                        
                                     Declaration of `nesting[]` at line 131, size evidently less than 63 bytes.                                                                                                 
                                     Fault at `json.c:186:28` during processing of a `{` or `[` character.                                                                                                      
                                - ASan report highlights the buffer region `[32,62)` as valid and shows the write at offset 62, just beyond the allocated redzone (`f1 f1 f1 f1`).                               
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             2. Patch attempt details                                                                                                                                                            
                                - Changes in `src/json.h`:                                                                                                                                                       
                                  ```diff                                                                                                                                                                        
                                  -#ifndef MG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH                                                                                                                                                     
                                  -#define MG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH 30                                                                                                                                                  
                                  +#ifndef MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING                                                                                                                                                   
                                  +#define MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING 60                                                                                                                                                
                                  #endif                                                                                                                                                                         
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                                  -#ifndef MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING                                                                                                                                                   
                                  -#define MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING 60                                                                                                                                                
                                  +#ifndef MG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH                                                                                                                                                     
                                  +#define MG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING                                                                                                                                 
                                  #endif                                                                                                                                                                         
                                  ```                                                                                                                                                                            
                                - Changes in `src/json.c` within `mg_json_get` around line 164:                                                                                                                  
                                  ```diff                                                                                                                                                                        
                                  -          if (depth > MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING) return MG_JSON_TOO_DEEP;                                                                                                           
                                  +          if (depth + 1 > (int)(sizeof(nesting) / sizeof(nesting[0])))                                                                                                        
                                  +            return MG_JSON_TOO_DEEP;                                                                                                                                          
                                  ```                                                                                                                                                                            
                                  and similarly for the `[` case.                                                                                                                                                
                                - Rebuild and rerun fuzzing: the same ASan error at `json.c:186` with identical overflow offset is observed.                                                                     
                                                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             3. Areas for further investigation                                                                                                                                                  
                                - The declaration and actual size of the `nesting` array in `mg_json_get` (around line 127 in `json.c`).                                                                         
                                - The logic calculating `depth`, `ed`, `ci`, `ei` and their interaction with `nesting`.                                                                                          
                                - The relationship between the `MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING`/`MG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH` macros and the static allocation of `nesting[]`.                                                        
                                - Any other code paths in `mg_json_get` that write to `nesting` without proper bounds checking.                                                                                  
                                - Header definitions in `json.h` to confirm whether macros are used consistently in all relevant checks.
