                             src/json.c:125-260                                                                                                                                                                  
                             ```                                                                                                                                                                                 
                             125:                                                                                                                                                                                
                             126:int mg_json_get(struct mg_str json, const char *path, int *toklen) {                                                                                                            
                             127:  const char *s = json.buf;                                                                                                                                                     
                             128:  int len = (int) json.len;                                                                                                                                                     
                             129:  enum { S_VALUE, S_KEY, S_COLON, S_COMMA_OR_EOO } expecting = S_VALUE;                                                                                                         
                             130:  unsigned char nesting[MG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH];                                                                                                                                     
                             131:  int i = 0;             // Current offset in `s`                                                                                                                               
                             132:  int j = 0;             // Offset in `s` we're looking for (return value)                                                                                                      
                             133:  int depth = 0;         // Current depth (nesting level)                                                                                                                       
                             134:  int ed = 0;            // Expected depth                                                                                                                                      
                             135:  int pos = 1;           // Current position in `path`                                                                                                                          
                             136:  int ci = -1, ei = -1;  // Current and expected index in array                                                                                                                 
                             137:                                                                                                                                                                                
                             138:  if (toklen) *toklen = 0;                                                                                                                                                      
                             139:  if (path[0] != '$') return MG_JSON_INVALID;                                                                                                                                   
                             140:                                                                                                                                                                                
                             141:#define MG_CHECKRET(x)                                  \                                                                                                                       
                             142:  do {                                                  \                                                                                                                       
                             143:    if (depth == ed && path[pos] == '\0' && ci == ei) { \                                                                                                                       
                             144:      if (toklen) *toklen = i - j + 1;                  \                                                                                                                       
                             145:      return j;                                         \                                                                                                                       
                             146:    }                                                   \                                                                                                                       
                             147:  } while (0)                                                                                                                                                                   
                             148:                                                                                                                                                                                
                             149:// In the ascii table, the distance between `[` and `]` is 2.                                                                                                                   
                             150:// Ditto for `{` and `}`. Hence +2 in the code below.                                                                                                                           
                             151:#define MG_EOO(x)                                            \                                                                                                                  
                             152:  do {                                                       \                                                                                                                  
                             153:    if (depth == ed && ci != ei) return MG_JSON_NOT_FOUND;   \                                                                                                                  
                             154:    if (c != nesting[depth - 1] + 2) return MG_JSON_INVALID; \                                                                                                                  
                             155:    depth--;                                                 \                                                                                                                  
                             156:    MG_CHECKRET(x);                                          \                                                                                                                  
                             157:  } while (0)                                                                                                                                                                   
                             158:                                                                                                                                                                                
                             159:  for (i = 0; i < len; i++) {                                                                                                                                                   
                             160:    unsigned char c = ((unsigned char *) s)[i];                                                                                                                                 
                             161:    if (c == ' ' || c == '\t' || c == '\n' || c == '\r') continue;                                                                                                              
                             162:    switch (expecting) {                                                                                                                                                        
                             163:      case S_VALUE:                                                                                                                                                             
                             164:        // p("V %s [%.*s] %d %d %d %d\n", path, pos, path, depth, ed, ci, ei);                                                                                                  
                             165:        if (depth == ed) j = i;                                                                                                                                                 
                             166:        if (c == '{') {                                                                                                                                                         
                             167:          if (depth > MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING) return MG_JSON_TOO_DEEP;                                                                                                             
                             168:          if (depth == ed && path[pos] == '.' && ci == ei) {                                                                                                                    
                             169:            // If we start the object, reset array indices                                                                                                                      
                             170:            ed++, pos++, ci = ei = -1;                                                                                                                                          
                             171:          }                                                                                                                                                                     
                             172:          nesting[depth++] = c;                                                                                                                                                 
                             173:          expecting = S_KEY;                                                                                                                                                    
                             174:          break;                                                                                                                                                                
                             175:        } else if (c == '[') {                                                                                                                                                  
                             176:          if (depth > MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING) return MG_JSON_TOO_DEEP;                                                                                                             
                             177:          if (depth == ed && path[pos] == '[' && ei == ci) {                                                                                                                    
                             178:            ed++, pos++, ci = 0;                                                                                                                                                
                             179:            for (ei = 0; path[pos] != ']' && path[pos] != '\0'; pos++) {                                                                                                        
                             180:              ei *= 10;                                                                                                                                                         
                             181:              ei += path[pos] - '0';                                                                                                                                            
                             182:            }                                                                                                                                                                   
                             183:            if (path[pos] != 0) pos++;                                                                                                                                          
                             184:          }                                                                                                                                                                     
                             185:          nesting[depth++] = c;                                                                                                                                                 
                             186:          break;                                                                                                                                                                
                             187:        } else if (c == ']' && depth > 0) {  // Empty array                                                                                                                     
                             188:          MG_EOO(']');                                                                                                                                                          
                             189:        } else if (c == 't' && i + 3 < len && memcmp(&s[i], "true", 4) == 0) {                                                                                                  
                             190:          i += 3;                                                                                                                                                               
                             191:        } else if (c == 'n' && i + 3 < len && memcmp(&s[i], "null", 4) == 0) {                                                                                                  
                             192:          i += 3;                                                                                                                                                               
                             193:        } else if (c == 'f' && i + 4 < len && memcmp(&s[i], "false", 5) == 0) {                                                                                                 
                             194:          i += 4;                                                                                                                                                               
                             195:        } else if (c == '-' || ((c >= '0' && c <= '9'))) {                                                                                                                      
                             196:          int numlen = 0;                                                                                                                                                       
                             197:          mg_atod(&s[i], len - i, &numlen);                                                                                                                                     
                             198:          i += numlen - 1;                                                                                                                                                      
                             199:        } else if (c == '"') {                                                                                                                                                  
                             200:          int n = mg_pass_string(&s[i + 1], len - i - 1);                                                                                                                       
                             201:          if (n < 0) return n;                                                                                                                                                  
                             202:          i += n + 1;                                                                                                                                                           
                             203:        } else {                                                                                                                                                                
                             204:          return MG_JSON_INVALID;                                                                                                                                               
                             205:        }                                                                                                                                                                       
                             206:        MG_CHECKRET('V');                                                                                                                                                       
                             207:        if (depth == ed && ei >= 0) ci++;                                                                                                                                       
                             208:        expecting = S_COMMA_OR_EOO;                                                                                                                                             
                             209:        break;                                                                                                                                                                  
                             210:                                                                                                                                                                                
                             211:      case S_KEY:                                                                                                                                                               
                             212:        if (c == '"') {                                                                                                                                                         
                             213:          int n = mg_pass_string(&s[i + 1], len - i - 1);                                                                                                                       
                             214:          if (n < 0) return n;                                                                                                                                                  
                             215:          if (i + 1 + n >= len) return MG_JSON_NOT_FOUND;                                                                                                                       
                             216:          if (depth < ed) return MG_JSON_NOT_FOUND;                                                                                                                             
                             217:          if (depth == ed && path[pos - 1] != '.') return MG_JSON_NOT_FOUND;                                                                                                    
                             218:          // printf("K %s [%.*s] [%.*s] %d %d %d %d %d\n", path, pos, path, n,                                                                                                  
                             219:          //        &s[i + 1], n, depth, ed, ci, ei);                                                                                                                           
                             220:          //  NOTE(cpq): in the check sequence below is important.                                                                                                              
                             221:          //  strncmp() must go first: it fails fast if the remaining length                                                                                                    
                             222:          //  of the path is smaller than `n`.                                                                                                                                  
                             223:          if (depth == ed && path[pos - 1] == '.' &&                                                                                                                            
                             224:              strncmp(&s[i + 1], &path[pos], (size_t) n) == 0 &&                                                                                                                
                             225:              (path[pos + n] == '\0' || path[pos + n] == '.' ||                                                                                                                 
                             226:               path[pos + n] == '[')) {                                                                                                                                         
                             227:            pos += n;                                                                                                                                                           
                             228:          }                                                                                                                                                                     
                             229:          i += n + 1;                                                                                                                                                           
                             230:          expecting = S_COLON;                                                                                                                                                  
                             231:        } else if (c == '}') {  // Empty object                                                                                                                                 
                             232:          MG_EOO('}');                                                                                                                                                          
                             233:          expecting = S_COMMA_OR_EOO;                                                                                                                                           
                             234:          if (depth == ed && ei >= 0) ci++;                                                                                                                                     
                             235:        } else {                                                                                                                                                                
                             236:          return MG_JSON_INVALID;                                                                                                                                               
                             237:        }                                                                                                                                                                       
                             238:        break;                                                                                                                                                                  
                             239:                                                                                                                                                                                
                             240:      case S_COLON:                                                                                                                                                             
                             241:        if (c == ':') {                                                                                                                                                         
                             242:          expecting = S_VALUE;                                                                                                                                                  
                             243:        } else {                                                                                                                                                                
                             244:          return MG_JSON_INVALID;                                                                                                                                               
                             245:        }                                                                                                                                                                       
                             246:        break;                                                                                                                                                                  
                             247:                                                                                                                                                                                
                             248:      case S_COMMA_OR_EOO:                                                                                                                                                      
                             249:        if (depth <= 0) {                                                                                                                                                       
                             250:          return MG_JSON_INVALID;                                                                                                                                               
                             251:        } else if (c == ',') {                                                                                                                                                  
                             252:          expecting = (nesting[depth - 1] == '{') ? S_KEY : S_VALUE;                                                                                                            
                             253:        } else if (c == ']' || c == '}') {                                                                                                                                      
                             254:          if (depth == ed && c == '}' && path[pos - 1] == '.')                                                                                                                  
                             255:            return MG_JSON_NOT_FOUND;                                                                                                                                           
                             256:          if (depth == ed && c == ']' && path[pos - 1] == ',')                                                                                                                  
                             257:            return MG_JSON_NOT_FOUND;                                                                                                                                           
                             258:          MG_EOO('O');                                                                                                                                                          
                             259:          if (depth == ed && ei >= 0) ci++;                                                                                                                                     
                             260:        } else {                                                                                                                                                                
                             ```
